let add : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @, n) => n 
    case (~succ m, n) => ~succ (self(m, n))

let leafCount : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => ( 
    case ~leaf @ => ~succ ~zero @
    case ~node(l, r) => (add)((self)(l), (self)(r))
)) in
@

let max : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @, n) => n 
    case (m, ~zero @) => m 
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let depth : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => ( 
    case ~leaf @ => ~succ ~zero @
    case ~node(l, r) => ~succ (max((self)(l), (self)(r)))
)) in

let even : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @) => ~true @
    case (~succ ~zero @) => ~false @
    case (~succ (~succ n)) => self(n)
)) in
let all_even : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => ( 
    case ~nil @ => ~true @
    case ~cons (x, xs) => 
        if (even)(x) then self(xs) else ~false @
)) in

let lte : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @, n) => ~true @ 
    case (~succ m, ~zero @) => ~false @ 
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => self(m, n) 
)) in

    case ~nil @ => ~true @
    case ~cons (x, ~nil @) => ~true @
    case ~cons (x, ~cons (y, ys)) => 
        if (lte)(x, y) then self(~cons (y, ys)) else ~false @
)) in
